reviewTitle valignMiddle"><strong>Very good for the amazing price</strong></a><span class="gry valignMiddle">        <span class="inlineblock txtsmall">September 30, 2014</span> </span></div>  <div class="mt4 ath"><span class="gr10">        <span class="txtsmall"><span class="gry">By</span> <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A238TJT03Z6A31/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/181-0609059-5377554" <div class="mt9 reviewText">       <div class="drkgry">   I have to say, I'm pretty happy with this controller. The price of it is unbeatable for an official Sony controller. I bought mine used and it feels fine. You can tell it's kinda old due to the plastic not having that oh so sweet new feeling to it, and the analog sticks are a bit worn, but not so much that it is really noticeable.<br /><br />Pros: It was cheap, it feels nice, all the buttons work perfectly.<br />Cons: The handles of the controller are a bit scuffed up, but it's not that big a deal. It doesn't come with a charger cord and the battery seems to die faster than my other PS3 controllers.<br /><br />All in all, I'd definitely recommend this. You can't beat this price. </div>  </div>  <div class="imageTiles" style="margin-top:5px">   </div>  <div class="clearboth txtsmall gt9 vtStripe">    <div class="fl cmt">     <a   <div class="clearboth"></div>    </div>  </div></div>            <div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpful-RO2WV5G1S61WO" class="reviews" style="margin-top:30px;">  <div class="gry txtsmall hlp">1 of 1 people found the following review helpful</div>  <div class="clearboth"></div>  <div class="mt4 ttl"><span class="swSprite s_star_5_0 " title="5.0 out of 5 stars" ><span>5.0 out of 5 stars</span></span>   <a href="http://www.amazon.com/review/RO2WV5G1S61WO/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/181-0609059-5377554?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00CUKPSGO&nodeID=468642&store=videogames" class="txtlarge gl3 gr4 reviewTitle valignMiddle"><strong>Video game or robot controller...</strong></a><span class="gry valignMiddle">        <span class="inlineblock txtsmall">June 22, 2014</span> </span></div>  <div class="mt4 ath"><span class="gr10">        <span class="txtsmall"><span class="gry">By</span> <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A2KOU7DP32TWEJ/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/181-0609059-5377554" class="noTextDecoration">John Wolf</a></span> </span>   </div>  <div class="txtsmall mt4 fvavp"><span class="inlineblock avpOrVine" ><span class="orange strong avp">Verified Purchase</span></span></div>  <div class="mt9 reviewText">       <div class="drkgry">   I bought the PS3 as a separate item to control a robot. I don't have the Playstation, so I was at risk. Turns out the PS3 is a perfect match with generic Bluetooth devices and pairs easily. Sony intends for you to have the Playstation as well so there is a trick to turning off the controller. Normally, you have to click a button on the Playstation screen to turn off the device, but if you hold the &#34;on&#34; button down for 10 seconds, it will turn off. Whew! This is critical. Otherwise you run the battery down on each use. The battery is charged via a mini-USB cable to any normal USB connection on any computer. It flashes four LEDs until charged, then they go out. At that point, hold the main button down for 10 seconds to ensure the unit is off. I had to push the &#34;on&#34; when I first got the unit before the charger engaged. After that, it charged each time I plug in the USB port. Don't leave the USB cable in when the unit is fully charged. LiPo batteries don't like that. </div>  </div>  <div class="imageTiles" style="margin-top:5px">   </div>  <div class="clearboth txtsmall gt9 vtStripe">    <div class="fl cmt">     <a
